<h3 class="sr-hotel__title " data-et-click="customGoal:OQRWSEcYC:4">
<a class="hotel_name_link url" data-et-click="
" href="/hotel/jp/hotel-grand-fine-garden-kyoto-minami.zh-tw.html?label=gen173nr-1DCAEoggJCAlhYSDNiBW5vcmVmaOcBiAEBmAEwuAEGyAEM2AED6AEBkgIBeagCAw;sid=4996667e149bfae490c17f2eb37eafa9;checkin=2017-09-13;checkout=2017-09-17;ucfs=1;srpvid=2f0026497cff0120;highlighted_blocks=36666103_89051953_0_0_0;all_sr_blocks=36666103_89051953_0_0_0;room1=A%2CA;hpos=40;dest_type=city;dest_id=-235402;srfid=fd9a53b1e97782027ab2166c829d2e1edefc0e12X390;from=searchresults;highlight_room=#hotelTmpl" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
